***gnocchi.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gnocchi.html>gnocchi</a> (40755)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:gnocchi.html>gnocchi</a></i>, plural of <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">gnocco</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:dumpling.html>dumpling</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">nocchio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knot (in wood)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lombardic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lombardic language">Lombardic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">knohha</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knuckle, bone, knot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knukǭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kneukaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tuber, knuckle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gnew-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knot, bundle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">knoche</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bone, knot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knochen</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">knoke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knuckle, knob, knot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">knoge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knuckle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">knuckle</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gnocchi.html>gnocchi</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:gnocchi.html>gnocchi</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gnocchis</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Italian pasta-like <a href = vnd.unilang:dumplings.html>dumplings</a> made of potato or semolina.</li></ol>

***god.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a> (212)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">got</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gudą</i>, from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰutós</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">invoked (one)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:gott.html>Gott</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">gud</i>.
</p>

***goddeloos.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:goddeloos.html>goddeloos</a> (34202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-loos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-less</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goddeloos.html>goddeloos</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goddeloos.html>goddelozer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goddeloos.html>goddeloos</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">goddeloost</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">atheistic</span>; <span class="Latn" lang="en">godless</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">godloos</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ongelovig.html>ongelovig</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">atheïstisch</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>evil and corrupted esp. due to the lack of faith; <span class="Latn" lang="en">godless</span>

***godheid.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:godheid.html>godheid</a> (39500)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">godheit</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gothet</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-hood, -ness, -ity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,
</p><p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">godhood</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">godhead</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gottheit</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:godheid.html>godheid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:godheden.html>godheden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:godheid.html>godheidje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A divinity, deity, male or female</li>
<li>(<i>often capitalized: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:godheid.html>Godheid</a></b></i>) The divine nature of <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>, notably in monotheistic theology</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goddelijkheid.html>goddelijkheid</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">godendom</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">godshuus</i>. </p>

***godverdomme.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:godverdomme.html>godverdomme</a> (1588)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Univerbation of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdoemen.html>verdoeme</a></i>. Literally meaning “God dammit, may <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> damn”. It expresses the wish that <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> damns something. The <i>-me</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not the pronoun <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the Dutch suffix to indicate a subjunctive.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Two possible origins have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> proposed:
</p>
<ul><li>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> verdore di</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">may <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> make you crazy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verdoren</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make crazy, to mislead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>A minced oath of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:godverdomme.html>godverdomme</a></i>.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> (49)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">goet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">guot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gōdaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰedʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">good</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voel.html>voel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I feel <b>good</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">correct</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">right</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">factually or morally</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:helaas.html>Helaas</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:antwoord.html>antwoord</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Unfortunately, that answer <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not <b>correct</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sommige.html>Sommige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verschil.html>verschil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>tussen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fout.html>fout</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Some people can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> see the difference between <b>right</b> and wrong.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>well
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:speelt.html>speelt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></b> tennis.</i> — He plays tennis well.</dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slecht</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Adverbs are the same as adjectives, so also the archaic adverb <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i> (<i>well</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now <i><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></i>, though it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still used in compounds, see <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.vandale.nl/vandale/opzoeken/woordenboek/?zoekwoord=wel"><a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> starting with "<a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a>" in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dale.html>Dale</a></i></a>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:goedkoop.html>goedkoop</a> (3320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">goetcoop</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:goeden.html>goeden</a> coop</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">good buy; good purchase</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">goodkoop</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">goedkeap</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">good chepe</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goedkoop.html>goedkoop</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goedkoper.html>goedkoper</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goedkoopst.html>goedkoopst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cheap, inexpensive, affordable</li>
<li>cheap <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of inferior quality or being uncharitable</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:goedkoop.html>goedkoop</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:handel.html>handel</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:laag.html>laag</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:prijs.html>prijs</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goedkoop.html>goedkoop</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hotel.html>hotel</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:figuurlijk.html>figuurlijk</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:eenvoudig.html>eenvoudig</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slecht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedacht.html>bedacht</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goedkope.html>goedkope</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:leugen.html>leugen</a>.</i> </li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontzettend.html>ontzettend</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goedkope.html>goedkope</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:truc.html>truc</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***goeiedag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:goeiedag.html>goeiedag</a> (8608)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection_2">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goeiedag.html>goeiedag</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goedendag.html>goedendag</a></i></span></span>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although commonly used in everyday writing, this spelling <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> considered incorrect by some, who favour <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goedendag.html>goedendag</a></i> instead. Regardless of spelling, the pronunciation of both <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> identical.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:verwante.html>Verwante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li>goeiendag, <a href = vnd.unilang:goededag.html>goededag</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:goedendag.html>goedendag</a></li></ul>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:goeiemorgen.html>goeiemorgen</a> (3154)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goeie.html>goeie</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>morgen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goeiemorgen.html>goeiemorgen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">proscribed</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> good morning</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although commonly used in everyday writing, this form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> considered incorrect by some, who favour the more formal <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goedemorgen.html>goedemorgen</a></i> instead.
</p>
</body> 
***goeienacht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:goeienacht.html>goeienacht</a> (13112)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goeienacht.html>goeienacht</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>good night</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although commonly used in everyday writing, this spelling <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> considered incorrect by some, who favour <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goedenacht.html>goedenacht</a></i> instead. Regardless of spelling, the pronunciation of both <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> identical.
</p>
</body>

***goggles.html

<p>Probably from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">goggle</i>, from the appearance it gives the wearer.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:goggles.html>goggles</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Protective eyewear set in a flexible frame to fit snugly against the face.</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:blinds.html>Blinds</a> for shying <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a>.</li></ol>

***gom.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gom.html>gom</a> (69811)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gomme</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">gomme</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gumma</i>, from earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:gummi.html>gummi</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cummi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gom.html>gom</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gom.html>gommen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gom.html>gommetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>gum, various viscous or sticky substances exuded by certain plants or produced synthetically.</li>
<li>an object made from/with it, especially:</li>
<li>an eraser, used to delete markings by rubbing off the ink etc.</li></ol>

***gondel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gondel.html>gondel</a> (20793)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">gondola</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Venetian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Venetian language">Venetian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="vec">góndoła</i>, which likely derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κοντούρα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kontoúra</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small tail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gondel.html>gondel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gondels.html>gondels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gondel.html>gondeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A gondola <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">Venetian boat</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li>A gondola of a cable car.</li>
<li>The gondola of a balloon.</li>
<li>A decorated boat used in boat <a href = vnd.unilang:parades.html>parades</a>.</li></ol>

***gone.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a> (30528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">gon</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">igon</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:gan.html>gan</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">ȝegan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">gān</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ġegān</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gānaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, past participle of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gāną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with West Germanic <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">gane</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">gien</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">gahn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gegaan.html>gegaan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">gegangen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">go</i></span></span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gon</i></span></span> or gon': short for <a href = vnd.unilang:gonna.html>gonna</a>, going to.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">goner</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">yesterday <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Away, having left.
<dl><dd><i>Are they <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></b> already?</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> No longer part of the present situation.
<dl><dd><i>Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> both trying to understand what Grandma says, she's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></b>.</i></dd>
<dd><i>He <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> be going out with us tonight. Now that he's engaged, he's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></b>.</i></dd>
<dd><i>Have you seen their revenue numbers? They're <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>No longer existing, having passed.
<dl><dd><i>The days of my youth are <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>Used up.
<dl><dd><i>I'm afraid all the coffee's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></b> at the <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>Dead.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Intoxicated to the point of being unaware of one's surroundings.
<ul><li><b>1991</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stephen_Fry" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Stephen Fry">Stephen Fry</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Liar_(novel)" class="extiw" title="w:The Liar (novel)">The Liar</a></i>, p. 41:
<dl><dd>...she put on a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of sing-song voice whenever she <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> pissed, it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> one of the <a href = vnd.unilang:signs.html>signs</a> that she <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> really <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></b>...</dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>Dude, look at <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>Jack</a>. He's completely <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Entirely given up to; infatuated with; used with <i>on</i>.
<dl><dd><i>He's totally <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></b> on her.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Excellent; wonderful.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Ago (used post-positionally).
<ul><li><b>1999</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_RR_Martin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:George RR Martin">George RR Martin</a>, <i>A Clash of Kings</i>, Bantam 2011, p. 491:
<dl><dd>Six <a href = vnd.unilang:nights.html>nights</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></b>, your brother fell upon my uncle Stafford, encamped with his host at a village called Oxcross not three days ride from Casterly Rock.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Weak; faint; feeling a sense of goneness.</li>
<li>Of an arrow: wide of the mark.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From Late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gonorrhoea</i> (perhaps <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gonorrhoe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gonorrhö</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γονόῥροια</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gonórhroia</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γόνος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gónos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sperm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ῥέω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rhéō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, due the mucus having <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> mistaken for semen.

***goochelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:goochelen.html>goochelen</a> (24949)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gokelen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gōkelen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goochelen.html>goochelen</a></strong>
